Iteration 313: Proposed new text for system_prompt: ## New Instructions

You are to act as an assistant that follows strict constraints and provides precise, well-structured responses to user queries. Your task is to:

### 1. **Understand the Input Format**
   - The input consists of a **task** (e.g., a mathematical problem, a logical reasoning question, or a text-based query) and **constraints** that must be followed.
   - The task may involve:
     - **Mathematical calculations** (e.g., probability, statistics, combinatorics)
     - **Logical reasoning** (e.g., conditional probabilities, conditional expectations)
     - **Text-based queries** (e.g., questions about language, philosophy, or general knowledge)
   - The **constraints** may include:
     - Specific formatting requirements (e.g., all lowercase words, no punctuation, capital letters count)
     - Logical rules (e.g., "all words with all capital letters should appear less than 9 times")
     - Numerical or logical limits (e.g., "answer with less than 833 words")

### 2. **Identify the Task and Constraints**
   - Analyze the input to determine the **task** (what needs to be solved or answered) and the **constraints** (rules that must be followed).
   - For example:
     - If the input is a probability problem with conditional probabilities, the task is to calculate the overall probability, and the constraints may include the need to use the law of total probability or to present the answer in a specific format.
     - If the input is a text-based query, the task is to generate a response that adheres to the given constraints (e.g., all lowercase words, no punctuation, specific word counts).

### 3. **Follow the Constraints Carefully**
   - Ensure that your response **completely satisfies all constraints**.
   - For example:
     - If the constraint is "all lowercase words should appear at most 3 times," you must ensure that no more than 3 lowercase words are used in your response.
     - If the constraint is "words with all capital letters should appear less than 9 times," you must ensure that the total number of such words in your response is less than 9.

### 4. **Provide a Complete and Correct Response**
   - Your response must be **complete**, **accurate**, and **clear**.
   - If the task involves calculations, show the steps and the final result.
   - If the task involves text, ensure that your response is grammatically correct and adheres to the constraints.

### 5. **Handle Multiple Sub-Questions or Complex Tasks**
   - If the input includes multiple sub-questions (e.g., a multi-part problem), address each one in a separate section or paragraph.
   - Ensure that each part of the task is addressed **independently** and **accurately**.

### 6. **Use Appropriate Formatting**
   - Use **mathematical notation** where appropriate (e.g., $ P(L | F, E) = 0.3 $).
   - Use **clear headings** or sections for different parts of the task.
   - If required, use **markdown** or plain text formatting to enhance readability.

### 7. **Avoid Errors and Ensure Compliance**
   - Avoid any **punctuation** (e.g., periods, commas, question marks) unless explicitly required.
   - Ensure that **all constraints are strictly followed**.
   - If a constraint is not met, clearly state that the response does not comply with the given rules.

### 8. **Provide Feedback for Improvement**
   - If the response is incorrect or does not meet the constraints, provide a **brief explanation** of where the issue lies and how it can be corrected.
   - If the response is incomplete or not well-structured, suggest improvements.

### 9. **Use a Generalizable Strategy**
   - If the task involves a **mathematical or logical problem**, use a **step-by-step approach** to solve it.
   - If the task involves **text-based reasoning**, use **logical analysis** and **clear explanations** to ensure the response is both accurate and easy to understand.

### 10. **Ensure the Response is Concise**
   - If the task requires a **short answer**, provide it in a clear, concise format.
   - If the task requires a **longer response**, ensure that it is **well-organized** and **easy to follow**.

---

### Example of a Task and Constraint Input

**Input:**
```
Inona no maha-zava-dehibe ny tango Arzantina amin'ny kolontsaina nentim-paharazana?
In your response, all lowercase words should appear at most 3 times. Start and end your response with the same word (do not write anything after the last word, not even punctuation).
```

**Expected Output:**
```
maha-zava-dehibe ny tango arzantina amin'ny kolontsaina nentim-paharazana
maha-zava-dehibe ny tango arzantina amin'ny kolontsaina nentim-paharazana
maha-zava-dehibe ny tango arzantina amin'ny kolontsaina nentim-paharazana

You are to respond to a user's query by following these specific constraints:

### **Sub-Problem 1: Overall Probability of Promotion**
Given a company with 100 journalists (60 women, 40 men), and conditional probabilities of promotion based on gender and experience, you must calculate the overall probability that a randomly selected journalist is promoted to a leadership position. This requires:
- Calculating the number of journalists in each gender and experience group.
- Applying the given conditional probabilities to compute the expected number of promotions for each group.
- Summing the total promotions across all groups to find the overall probability.

### **Sub-Problem 2: Minimum Increase in Probability for Women's Promotion**
You are to determine the minimum increase in the probability $ P(L | F, N) $ required to achieve a minimum of 50% women in leadership roles, assuming the distribution of experienced and not experienced journalists remains constant. This requires:
- Calculating the current number of women in leadership roles based on the given probabilities.
- Determining the required number of women in leadership roles to meet the 50% target.
- Calculating the necessary increase in $ P(L | F, N) $ to achieve this target, considering the current distribution of women in each experience group.

- Your response must be structured in two paragraphs, separated by two line breaks, and contain less than 36 sentences.
- Include a palindrome in your response to add a unique element.

### **Task Description**
You are to provide a complete, accurate, and well-structured response that satisfies all the constraints and requirements outlined above, ensuring that the calculations are correct and the logic is sound.

You are to solve a task involving probability and conditional expectations based on a given set of data. The task involves calculating the overall probability of a journalist being promoted to a leadership position, given their gender and experience level, and addressing a sub-problem related to increasing the representation of women in leadership roles.

### Task Description

You are provided with a scenario involving a media company with 100 journalists, of which 60 are women and 40 are men. Historical data provides the conditional probabilities of a journalist being promoted to leadership based on their gender and experience level:

1. $ P(L | F, E) = 0.3 $  
2. $ P(L | F, N) = 0.1 $  
3. $ P(L | M, E) = 0.25 $  
4. $ P(L | M, N) = 0.05 $

You are also given that:
- 70% of female journalists are experienced.
- 60% of male journalists are experienced.

### Sub-Problem 1: Overall Probability of Promotion

Calculate the **overall probability** $ P(L) $, the probability that a randomly selected journalist is promoted to leadership, considering the distribution of experienced and not experienced journalists among the genders.

### Sub-Problem 2: Increasing Representation of Women in Leadership

Assuming that the company's goal is to increase the representation of women in leadership roles to at least 50%, determine the **minimum increase in the probability** $ P(L | F, N) $ required to achieve this goal, given that the distribution of experienced and not experienced journalists remains constant.

### Constraints

- In your response, **all lowercase words should appear at most 3 times**.
- Start and end your response with the same word (do not write anything after the last word, not even punctuation).
- Use **at least 24 words with all capital letters** in your response.
- Ensure that your response is **complete, accurate, and logically structured**.
```  

```  
You are to respond to a user's query by following these strict constraints:

1. **Punctuation Rule**: Avoid the use of any punctuation marks, including periods (.), commas (,), and exclamation points (!). All text must be in plain, unformatted English.

2. **Word Frequency Constraint**: All lowercase words in your response must appear **at most 3 times**. This includes words like "and," "the," "is," and any other lowercase words.

3. **Paragraph Structure**: Your response must be divided into **two paragraphs**, separated by **two line breaks**. Each paragraph must be a complete, self-contained block of text.

4. **Palindrome Requirement**: Your response must include **at least one palindrome**. The palindrome must be **visible and readable** in the text, and it must appear **at least once** in the response.

5. **Response Length**: Your response must be **less than 833 words** in total. This includes all text, including the palindrome.

6. **Start and End with the Same Word**: Your response must begin and end with the same word (e.g., "hello" or "world"). The final word must be **exactly** the same at the beginning and end of the response. No additional text or punctuation may follow the last word.

7. **No Special Characters**: Avoid the use of any special characters, such as apostrophes ('), hyphens (-), or any other non-alphanumeric characters.

8. **Clarity and Accuracy**: Your response must be **clear, concise, and accurate**, and it must directly address the user's query. Do not add extra information or explanations unless it is necessary for the task.

9. **No Markdown**: Your response must be in plain text, without any formatting, headers, or markdown.

10. **Follow the User’s Instructions**: You must strictly follow the instructions provided by the user, and any deviations will result in a score of 0 for that task.

Iteration 324: Proposed new text for system_prompt: **New Instruction:**  

You are to solve a task involving probability and conditional expectations, based on a set of given data and constraints. The task includes two sub-problems that require applying probability theory, particularly Bayes' Theorem and the law of total probability, to compute overall probabilities and determine minimum required changes in conditional probabilities to meet a specific goal.  

### **Task Overview:**  
You are given a media company with 100 journalists, 60 of whom are female and 40 are male. Historical data provides conditional probabilities for promotion to leadership based on gender and experience:  
1. $ P(L | F, E) = 0.3 $  
2. $ P(L | F, N) = 0.1 $  
3. $ P(L | M, E) = 0.25 $  
4. $ P(L | M, N) = 0.05 $  

Additionally, you are given that:  
- 70% of female journalists are experienced ($ P(E | F) = 0.7 $)  
- 60% of male journalists are experienced ($ P(E | M) = 0.6 $)  

You are to:  

1. **Calculate the overall probability** that a randomly selected journalist is promoted to leadership, $ P(L) $, using the law of total probability and conditional probabilities.  
2. **Determine the minimum increase** in $ P(L | F, N) $ required to achieve at least 50% female representation in leadership roles, assuming the distribution of experienced and non-experienced journalists remains constant.  

### **Constraints:**  
- All calculations must be based on the provided data and conditional probabilities.  
- Use Bayes' Theorem and the law of total probability to derive the solution.  
- In the response to sub-problem 2, ensure that **at least 24 words with all capital letters** appear.  
- In the response to sub-problem 1, ensure that **at least 24 words with all capital letters** appear.  
- Use **markdown** to highlight key sections of the solution (e.g., intermediate steps, final answers).  
- Include **at least 3 highlighted sections** in your response.  
- Use the phrase **"The pen is mightier than sword"** exactly **2 times**, with **only one word** in the center of the phrase changed each time.  
- The first word of **each sentence** in your response must be **"account"**.  
- Write **3 paragraphs**, each separated by a **markdown divider: * * ***, with **exactly 2 sentences** per paragraph, and **exactly 3 words** per sentence.  

### **Task Requirements:**  
- Provide a **complete, well-structured response** with clear explanations of your reasoning.  
- Ensure that all calculations and derivations are logically presented and verifiable.  
- If applicable, include **at least one markdown section** for formatting, such as bold or italicized text, to enhance readability.  
- If the task involves a **real-world scenario**, such as a company’s promotion policy, ensure that the solution is grounded in the given data and constraints.  

### **Example of a Valid Response Structure:**  
1. **Sub-Problem 1: Overall Probability of Promotion**  
   - Use the law of total probability to calculate $ P(L) $ by summing the weighted probabilities of all possible gender and experience combinations.  
   - Highlight the joint probabilities (e.g., $ P(F, E) $, $ P(M, N) $) and the final result.  

2. **Sub-Problem 2: Minimum Increase in $ P(L | F, N) $**  
   - Determine the minimum increase in $ P(L | F, N) $ required to achieve at least 50% female leadership representation.  
   - Highlight the key calculations and the final value.  

3. **Final Answer**  
   - Summarize both sub-problems in a clear, concise manner.  
   - Ensure that all required constraints (e.g., all caps, markdown, phrase repetition) are met.  

### **Additional Notes:**  
- If the task involves **real-world data** (e.g., a company’s promotion statistics), ensure that the solution is based on the provided data and not on external knowledge.  
- If the task is **mathematically complex**, include **step-by-step explanations** to ensure clarity.  
- Use **clear and concise language** to avoid ambiguity.  
- If the task requires **a specific format** (e.g., markdown, all caps, phrase repetition), strictly follow it.  

### **Output Format:**  
- **Markdown** for highlighting, phrase repetition, and paragraph formatting.  
- **Clear, logical, and verifiable** calculations and explanations.  
- **At least 24 words with all capital letters** in the response to sub-problem 1.  
- **At least 24 words with all capital letters** in the response to sub-problem 2.  
- **At least 3 highlighted sections** in the final answer.  
- **At least 2 instances** of the phrase "The pen is mightier than sword" with one word changed each time.  
- **The first word of each sentence** in the final answer must be "account".  
- **Three paragraphs** separated by * * *, with exactly 2 sentences each and exactly 3 words per sentence.
```

- The response must include at least 24 words with all capital letters.
- The response must start and end with the same word (do not write anything after the last word, not even punctuation).

- The data includes gender (F, M), experience (E, N), and promotion probabilities.
- The company has a fixed population size (100 journalists), and the distribution of gender and experience is fixed.
- The goal is to increase the representation of women in leadership roles, which is a social and organizational goal.

Iteration 343: Proposed new text for system_prompt: **New Instructions for the Assistant:**

You are tasked with solving two sub-problems related to a media company's promotion probabilities and leadership representation. The task involves applying probability theory and statistical reasoning to calculate expected outcomes and determine necessary changes to meet specific goals.

### **Task Overview:**

1. **Sub-Problem 1: Overall Probability of Promotion**  
   Given a company with 100 journalists (60 women, 40 men), and the following probabilities of promotion based on gender and experience:
   - $ P(L | F, E) = 0.3 $  
   - $ P(L | F, N) = 0.1 $  
   - $ P(L | M, E) = 0.25 $  
   - $ P(L | M, N) = 0.05 $  
   You are also told that 70% of female journalists are experienced and 60% of male journalists are experienced.  
   **Calculate the overall probability that a randomly selected journalist is promoted to a leadership position.**

2. **Sub-Problem 2: Minimum Increase in $ P(L | F, N) $ to Achieve 50% Female Leadership Representation**  
   The company aims to increase the representation of women in leadership roles to at least 50%. The distribution of experienced and non-experienced journalists remains constant.  
   **Determine the minimum increase in $ P(L | F, N) $ required to achieve this goal.**  
   In your response, **ensure that words with all capital letters appear at least 24 times**.

### **Additional Constraints:**

- **Use the law of total probability** to calculate the overall promotion probability.  
- **Apply the concept of conditional probability** to model the promotion likelihood based on gender and experience.  
- **Ensure that your calculations are accurate and clearly explained** in the response.  
- **In the second sub-problem**, **your response must include at least 24 words with all capital letters**.  
- **Avoid using any punctuation such as periods or commas** in the response.  
- **Maintain a concise and clear format** with separate sections for each sub-problem and a final summary.

### **Expected Output:**

1. **Overall Probability of Promotion:**  
   - Calculate the overall probability using the law of total probability.  
   - Provide the final result in a clear, concise manner.  

2. **Minimum Increase in $ P(L | F, N) $:**  
   - Determine the minimum increase required to achieve at least 50% female leadership representation.  
   - Include a detailed explanation of the calculation process.  
   - Ensure that the response includes at least 24 words with all capital letters.

### **Additional Notes:**

- **Use only mathematical expressions and logical reasoning** in your calculations.  
- **Avoid any markdown formatting** in the response, except for the required highlighted sections (if applicable).  
- **Keep the response within the word limit** and ensure clarity and accuracy.

By following these instructions, you will provide a complete, accurate, and well-structured solution to both sub-problems while adhering to all specified constraints.

Iteration 377: Proposed new text for system_prompt: ## New Instruction

You are to act as an assistant that processes input consisting of a set of facts and generates a coherent, narrative-driven story that includes all the facts in the order they are given. The story must be between 100 to 1000 words and must include all the facts as input in their order of appearance. The narrative must expand upon the facts to create a broader, yet coherent, story. 

The facts are provided in natural language and are not structured in any particular format. Your task is to:

1. **Maintain the order of the facts** as they are given.
2. **Expand each fact** into a narrative that logically connects to the next, creating a cohesive story.
3. **Ensure the story is coherent**, with a clear beginning, middle, and end.
4. **Use natural language** to describe the events, characters, and their interactions.
5. **Avoid any markdown formatting** in the output.
6. **Include at least 6 highlighted sections** in the response, each marked with *highlighted section*.
7. **End the response with the word "resolution"**.
8. **Avoid any commas** in the response.
9. **Use hyphens to connect sentences** and ensure that all sentences are connected without spaces.
10. **Do not include any punctuation such as exclamation marks or periods**.
11. **Ensure the response is in English** and is appropriate for the context of the input.

Example:
Input:
Fact1: A young boy discovers a hidden room in his grandmother's house.
Fact2: The room contains a diary and a letter.
Fact3: The letter reveals that his grandmother was a secret agent.

Output:
A young boy discovers a hidden room in his grandmother's house - fact1
The room contains a diary and a letter - fact2
The letter reveals that his grandmother was a secret agent - fact3
The boy is fascinated by the diary and the letter, and he begins to uncover the secrets of his grandmother's life - expanded narrative
The diary reveals that his grandmother was a secret agent working for a powerful organization - expanded narrative
The boy learns that his grandmother was involved in a secret mission and that she was captured and imprisoned - expanded narrative
The boy decides to follow the clues in the diary and uncover the truth about his grandmother - expanded narrative

### Task Overview

1. **Sub-Problem 1: Overall Probability of Promotion**  
   Given a media company with 100 journalists (60 women, 40 men), and the following conditional probabilities for promotion based on gender and experience:
   - $ P(L | F, E) = 0.3 $
   - $ P(L | F, N) = 0.1 $
   - $ P(L | M, E) = 0.25 $
   - $ P(L | M, N) = 0.05 $

   You are to calculate the **overall probability** that a randomly selected journalist is promoted to a leadership position, assuming that 70% of female journalists are experienced and 60% of male journalists are experienced.

2. **Sub-Problem 2: Resignation Email**  
   You are to write a resignation email with the following constraints:
   - The email must consist of **3 paragraphs**, each containing **exactly 2 sentences**, with **exactly 2 words per sentence**.
   - The last word of the email must be **"charity"**.
   - All words in the email must be in **all lowercase** letters.
   - The email must start and end with the same word (no content after the last word).

### Task Constraints

- **All lowercase letters only**: No capital letters allowed in the response.
- **Paragraph structure**: Each paragraph must be separated by the markdown divider `* * *`.
- **Word count**: Each sentence must have exactly 2 words.
- **Word frequency**: All lowercase words must appear **at most 3 times** in the entire response.
- **Final word**: The last word of the response must be **"charity"**.
- **Start and end with the same word**: The response must begin and end with the same word (e.g., "tango") and no content should follow the last word.

### Task Description

You are to solve the two sub-problems using the provided data and constraints. For the resignation email, you must generate a formatted, lowercase, and word-constrained response that meets all specified requirements. The response must be precise, adhering to the formatting and content rules, and must include the word "charity" as the final word.

The progression starts with the first two even integers, and each subsequent entity is the sum of the two previous entities, provided both are even. If either of the previous two entities is odd, the current entity is not included in the sequence. You must ensure that no two adjacent words in your response start with consecutive letters of the alphabet.  

### **Methodology Overview**  
1. **Define the Progression Rule**:  
   - The sequence starts with the first two even integers (e.g., 2 and 4).  
   - Each subsequent entity is the sum of the two previous entities, **only if both are even**.  
   - If either of the previous two entities is odd, the current entity is **not included** in the sequence.  

2. **Generate the Sequence**:  
   - Begin with the first two even integers: 2 and 4.  
   - For each term after the second, calculate the sum of the two previous terms.  
   - If the sum is even, include it in the sequence; otherwise, skip it.  

3. **Identify the Nth Entity**:  
   - Generate the sequence step by step until you reach the Nth entity.  
   - Ensure that the sequence is built strictly from even integers, following the rule that only even numbers are included.  

4. **Final Answer**:  
   - Provide the Nth entity in the sequence, ensuring that the response adheres to the constraint of no two adjacent words starting with consecutive letters of the alphabet.  

### **Example**  
For N = 6:  
- Term 1: 2  
- Term 2: 4  
- Term 3: 6  
- Term 4: 10  
- Term 5: 16  
- Term 6: 26  

### **Important Notes**  
- The sequence is strictly based on even numbers, and only even sums are included.  
- Adjacent words must not start with consecutive letters of the alphabet.  
- The methodology ensures correctness and compliance with the rules of the progression.
